Booking Process

Step 1

Explore your city

Discover the housing options different cities have to offer as you plan for life at college.

Step 2

Submit an application

Apply for any properties that meet your needs. We’ll be there every step of the way to guide you through any paperwork required.

Step 3

Confirm your booking

Lease signed and any pre-payments made, you’re ready to embark on an exciting phase of life!

Explore

## University of Leeds

## Yorkshire’s largest and oldest university, Leeds is a dynamic and highly respected institution with an active, energetic student union

The University of Leeds is an internationally renowned university, 10 minutes from the city centre, with origins dating back to the 1830s. It boasts one of the UK’s best student unions and world-class facilities including The Edge, a state-of-the-art fitness and wellbeing centre. Choose to live in the north of the city centre or in the Woodhouse and Headingley area of town for an easy commute.

About

## Yorkshire’s largest and oldest university, Leeds is a dynamic and highly respected institution with an active, energetic student union

The University of Leeds is an internationally renowned university, 10 minutes from the city centre, with origins dating back to the 1830s. It boasts one of the UK’s best student unions and world-class facilities including The Edge, a state-of-the-art fitness and wellbeing centre. Choose to live in the north of the city centre or in the Woodhouse and Headingley area of town for an easy commute.

Explore University of Leeds

About

## Yorkshire’s largest and oldest university, Leeds is a dynamic and highly respected institution with an active, energetic student union

The University of Leeds is an internationally renowned university, 10 minutes from the city centre, with origins dating back to the 1830s. It boasts one of the UK’s best student unions and world-class facilities including The Edge, a state-of-the-art fitness and wellbeing centre. Choose to live in the north of the city centre or in the Woodhouse and Headingley area of town for an easy commute.

## University of Leeds

## Yorkshire’s largest and oldest university, Leeds is a dynamic and highly respected institution with an active, energetic student union

The University of Leeds is an internationally renowned university, 10 minutes from the city centre, with origins dating back to the 1830s. It boasts one of the UK’s best student unions and world-class facilities including The Edge, a state-of-the-art fitness and wellbeing centre. Choose to live in the north of the city centre or in the Woodhouse and Headingley area of town for an easy commute.

## University of Leeds

## Yorkshire’s largest and oldest university, Leeds is a dynamic and highly respected institution with an active, energetic student union

The University of Leeds is an internationally renowned university, 10 minutes from the city centre, with origins dating back to the 1830s. It boasts one of the UK’s best student unions and world-class facilities including The Edge, a state-of-the-art fitness and wellbeing centre. Choose to live in the north of the city centre or in the Woodhouse and Headingley area of town for an easy commute.

## University of Leeds

## Yorkshire’s largest and oldest university, Leeds is a dynamic and highly respected institution with an active, energetic student union

The University of Leeds is an internationally renowned university, 10 minutes from the city centre, with origins dating back to the 1830s. It boasts one of the UK’s best student unions and world-class facilities including The Edge, a state-of-the-art fitness and wellbeing centre. Choose to live in the north of the city centre or in the Woodhouse and Headingley area of town for an easy commute.

## University of Leeds

## Yorkshire’s largest and oldest university, Leeds is a dynamic and highly respected institution with an active, energetic student union

The University of Leeds is an internationally renowned university, 10 minutes from the city centre, with origins dating back to the 1830s. It boasts one of the UK’s best student unions and world-class facilities including The Edge, a state-of-the-art fitness and wellbeing centre. Choose to live in the north of the city centre or in the Woodhouse and Headingley area of town for an easy commute.

function extractAssignedObject7(text, marker){
  const startMarker=text.indexOf(marker);
  if(startMarker<0) throw new Error('marker not found');
  const eq=text.indexOf('=', startMarker);
  const start=text.indexOf('{', eq);
  let depth=0, inStr=false, esc=false, quote='';
  for(let i=start;i<text.length;i++){
    const ch=text[i];
    if(inStr){
      if(esc){ esc=false; }
      else if(ch==='\\'){ esc=true; }
      else if(ch===quote){ inStr=false; }
    } else {
      if(ch==='"' || ch==="'"){ inStr=true; quote=ch; }
      else if(ch==='{') depth++;
      else if(ch==='}') { depth--; if(depth===0) return text.slice(start,i+1); }
    }
  }
  throw new Error('no end');
}

async function fetchArchive8(pg){
 const suffix=pg===1?'':'/pg'+pg;
 const url=`https://web.archive.org/web/20240222083453id_/https://www.student.com/uk/leeds/u/university-of-leeds${suffix}`;
 const res=await fetch(url);
 const txt=await res.text();
 console.log('pg',pg,'status',res.status,'url',res.url,'len',txt.length,'props',(txt.match(/property-card-new__/g)||[]).length,'show', (txt.match(/Show [0-9]+\s*(?:properties|Properties)/)||[''])[0]);
 return {pg,url:res.url,status:res.status,txt};
}
const pages8=[];
for(let pg=1;pg<=6;pg++) pages8.push(await fetchArchive8(pg));
function cleanHtml8(s){return s.replace(/<script[\s\S]*?<\/script>/gi,'').replace(/<style[\s\S]*?<\/style>/gi,'').replace(/<[^>]+>/g,' ').replace(/&nbsp;/g,' ').replace(/&#x27;/g,"'").replace(/&amp;/g,'&').replace(/\s+/g,' ').trim();}
function extractAttr8(block, attr){ const m=block.match(new RegExp(attr+'="([^"]*)"')); return m?m[1]:''; }
function parseCards8(pageObj){
 const parts=pageObj.txt.split('<div class="property-card-new">').slice(1);
 return parts.map((part,idx)=>{
   const block=part.split('<div class="property-card-new">')[0];
   const titleMatch=block.match(/class="property-card-link property-card-new__title"[^>]*>([\s\S]*?)<\/a>/);
   const title=titleMatch?cleanHtml8(titleMatch[1]):'';
   const hrefMatch=block.match(/<a href="([^"]+)"[^>]*class="property-card-link property-card-new__title"/);
   const href=hrefMatch?hrefMatch[1]:'';
   const text=cleanHtml8(block);
   const bills=[...text.matchAll(/Bills included: ([^£]+?)(?=(?:University of Leeds|\d+ min|Private Room|Entire Place|Shared Room|Sold out|Not available|View rooms|Map|$))/g)].map(m=>m[1].trim());
   const hasWifi=/Bills included:[^£]*(Wi-Fi|WiFi)/i.test(text);
   const hasCleaning=/Bills included:[^£]*Cleaning Service/i.test(text);
   const sold=/Sold out\s*on Student\.com/i.test(text);
   const notAvail=/Not available\s*on Student\.com/i.test(text);
   const unavailable=sold||notAvail;
   const prices=[];
   for(const rm of text.matchAll(/(Entire Place|Private Room|Shared Room)\s*£([0-9]+(?:\.[0-9]+)?)/g)) prices.push({type:rm[1],price:parseFloat(rm[2])});
   const from=text.match(/(?:From\s*)?£([0-9]+(?:\.[0-9]+)?)\s*\/week/i);
   const walk=(text.match(/University of Leeds\s*\|\s*Walk\s*([0-9]+\s*min)/i)||text.match(/(\d+ min)\s+\d+ min(?:\s+\d+ min)?/i)||[])[1]||'';
   return {pg:pageObj.pg,idx,title,href,text:text.slice(0,800),bills,hasWifi,hasCleaning,unavailable,prices,from:from?parseFloat(from[1]):null,walk};
 }).filter(c=>c.title);
}
const cards8=pages8.flatMap(parseCards8);
console.log('cards',cards8.length);
const candidates8=cards8.filter(c=>c.hasWifi&&c.hasCleaning&&!c.unavailable&&c.prices.some(p=>p.type==='Entire Place'))

## Things to know

Booking Process

Submit enquiry

Confirmed by the property manager

Making payment

Check in

Submit enquiry

Your booking will be automatically cancelled if the property manager doesn't accept within 72 hours.

You can contact the property manager via live chat to help you track the progress.

Confirmed by the property manager

You need to make the payment in time once the property manager confirms your booking.

If the property is not available, the property manager will give you a new offer trying the best to provide you with a similar property.

Making payment

You need to make a partial payment to confirm your booking.

Check in

Please wait for check-in in peace of mind after you complete the payment. (No more operations are required.)

House rules

These rules will need to be followed when you move in

No Pets

No Alcohol in Communal/Public Areas

Family Friendly

No under 18

No Smoking

---

## Your Bills

All inclusive bills

The price is the final price, no other fees added

-   Cleaning Service
-   Wifi
-   Water
-   Contents Insurance
-   Electricity
-   Heating
-   Gas

Tips: Facilities and fares are subject to the final contract.

---

## Cancellation policy - 

30 days cancellation period

Payment made

Cancel the booking within cancellation period

If you cancel the booking within the cancellation period

Any deposits/fees paid will be refunded

Any rental payments paid will be refunded

The transaction fee will not be refunded

The transaction fee is charged by the third payment platform (such as Stripe/Paypal) or the bank. If the booking is cancelled, the transaction fee is nonrefundable

30 calendar days before move in

Non-refundable

You can contact the property manager directly for more details.

Any payments made will not be refunded if you cancel outside the cancellation period

Move in

## Things to know

Booking Process

Submit enquiry

Confirmed by the property manager

Making payment

Check in

Submit enquiry

Your booking will be automatically cancelled if the property manager doesn't accept within 72 hours.

You can contact the property manager via live chat to help you track the progress.

Confirmed by the property manager

You need to make the payment in time once the property manager confirms your booking.

If the property is not available, the property manager will give you a new offer trying the best to provide you with a similar property.

Making payment

You need to make a partial payment to confirm your booking.

Check in

Please wait for check-in in peace of mind after you complete the payment. (No more operations are required.)

House rules

These rules will need to be followed when you move in

No Smoking

No under 18

No Pets

No Alcohol in Communal/Public Areas

Family Friendly

## Your Bills

All inclusive bills

The price is the final price, no other fees added

-   Cleaning Service
-   Wifi
-   Water
-   Contents Insurance
-   Electricity
-   Heating
-   Gas

Tips: Facilities and fares are subject to the final contract.

## Cancellation policy - 

30 days cancellation period

Payment made

Cancel the booking within cancellation period

If you cancel the booking within the cancellation period

Any deposits/fees paid will be refunded

Any rental payments paid will be refunded

The transaction fee will not be refunded

The transaction fee is charged by the third payment platform (such as Stripe/Paypal) or the bank. If the booking is cancelled, the transaction fee is nonrefundable

30 calendar days before move in

Non-refundable

You can contact the property manager directly for more details.

Any payments made will not be refunded if you cancel outside the cancellation period

Move in
